TITLE      Tabulated Cross Sections For Hydrogen and Helium       O029000100003 
           Particles Produced by 62 and 39 MeV Protons on 209-Bi  O029000100004 
AUTHOR     (F.E.BERTRAND,R.W.PEELLE)                              O029000100005 
REFERENCE  (R,ORNL-4638,197101)                                   O029000100006 
           (J,PR/C,8,1045,1973) Combined Paper Where the Data For O029000100007 
           Some Targets were Collected.                           O029000100008 
INSTITUTE  (1USAORL)                                              O029000100009 
FACILITY   (ISOCY) Oak Ridge Isochronous Cyclotron.               O029000100010 
           (SPECM) Momentum Analyzed in a 153 Degree Magnet.      O029000100011 
INC-SPECT  .Monoenergetic 60.5 - 61.9 +/- 0.1 and 38.7 +/- 0.1 MeVO029000100012 
            Protons, Focused on the Target in a Spot of Approxi-  O029000100013 
            Mately 8 mm Diameter, with a Walk of +/- 0.4 Cm. The  O029000100014 
            Uncertainty in Number of Protons Striking the Target  O029000100015 
            Was +/- 1%.                                           O029000100016 
METHOD     (EDE) The Secondary Particle Type was Identified with  O029000100017 
           (TOF) A Combination of Delta-E Versus E and Flight-TimeO029000100018 
           Versus E, Which Permitted Unambiguous Identification   O029000100019 
           From a Few MeV Up to 62 MeV. The Low-Energy            O029000100020 
           Cutoffs For the Different Particles were               O029000100021 
           -------------------------------------------------------O029000100022 
             61.7 MeV                                             O029000100023 
                  Protons       15 -  45 Degrees    6 - 9 MeV     O029000100024 
                                50 - 135 Degrees        4 MeV     O029000100025 
                                     160 Degrees        8 MeV     O029000100026 
                  Deuterons     15 - 135 Degrees        5 MeV     O029000100027 
                                     160 Degrees       11 MeV     O029000100028 
                  Tritons       15 - 135 Degrees        6 MeV     O029000100029 
                                     160 Degrees       13 MeV     O029000100030 
                  Helium-3      15 - 160 Degrees       14 MeV     O029000100031 
                  Alphas        15 - 160 Degrees       14 MeV     O029000100032 
            ------------------------------------------------------O029000100033 
             38.7 MeV                                             O029000100034 
                  Protons       20 -  45 Degrees        6 MeV     O029000100035 
                                      90 Degrees        4 MeV     O029000100036 
                  Deuterons     20 -  90 Degrees        5 MeV     O029000100037 
                  Tritons       20 -  90 Degrees        6 MeV     O029000100038 
                  Alphas        20 -  90 Degrees       14 MeV     O029000100039 
           -------------------------------------------------------O029000100040 
DETECTOR   (TELES,SOLST,GELI) A Solid State Three-Detector        O029000100041 
            Telescope, with Two Silicon Delta-E Detectors and a   O029000100042 
            Lithium-Drifted Germanium Detector Used For Total     O029000100043 
            Energy Absorption. The Total Resolution was           O029000100044 
           Approximately 180 KeV For Most of the Data.            O029000100045 
           The  Delta-E  Detectors  had Thicknesses of 100 and 500O029000100046 
           Micrometers.                                           O029000100047 
            The Telescope was Mounted in a Scattering Chamber withO029000100048 
            1.2 M Diameter. For the Runs at 61.7 MeV, Nickel      O029000100049 
            Collimators with a Thickness of 0.653 Cm and Areas of O029000100050 
            0.173 - 0.259 Cm2 +/- 1.5 %, was Used. For the        O029000100051 
            Runs at 38.7 MeV an Active Ne102 Collimator, with a   O029000100052 
            Thickness of 0.1 Cm and an Area of 0.342 Cm2 +/- 1.5%,O029000100053 
            Was Used. The Distance from the Target to the         O029000100054 
            Collimator was About 47 Cm +/- 1%. The Collimator     O029000100055 
            Had a Misalignment at the Center of the Scattering    O029000100056 
            Chamber of +/- 0.5 Cm. The Precision of the Detector  O029000100057 
            Angle was +/- 0.5 Degrees. The Zero Angle was         O029000100058 
            Determined to +/- 0.5 Degrees. The Angular Resolution O029000100059 
            Was Better Than +/- 0.45 Degrees.                     O029000100060 
SAMPLE     .Bismuth Target, 10.3 +/- 0.2 Mg/Cm2 Thick, with a     O029000100061 
            Thickness Nonuniformity of +/- 3 %. The Target        O029000100062 
            Contained 0.20 +/- 0.02 Atom % Carbon and             O029000100063 
            0.30 +/- 0.04 Atom % Oxygen. The Sample was           O029000100064 
            Oriented with an Angular Precision of +/- 0.5 Degrees.O029000100065 
CORRECTION .The Data were Corrected For                           O029000100066 
            1. Energy Loss of the Secondary Particles in the      O029000100067 
               Target,                                            O029000100068 
            2. Collimator Edge Penetration,                       O029000100069 
            3. Multiple Scattering of Particles in the First Two  O029000100070 
               Detectors, Which Made Them Miss the Total Absorp-  O029000100071 
               Tion Detector,                                     O029000100072 
            4. The Nickel Window Dead Layer of the Ge-Detector,   O029000100073 
               And,                                               O029000100074 
            5. Nuclear Reactions in the Ge-Detector.              O029000100075 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-S) Statistical Error in Data.                     O029000100076 
           (ERR-1) Systematic Error in Data, with Contributions   O029000100077 
            Such As                                               O029000100078 
            1. Uncertainty in Various Corrections  +/- 2 %        O029000100079 
            2. Uncertainty in Number of Protons                   O029000100080 
               Striking the Target                 +/- 1 %        O029000100081 
            3. Uncertainty in Dead Time            +/- 2 %        O029000100082 
           (EN-ERR) Uncertainty Beam Energy.                      O029000100083
